marched towardes oldemerct to expulse the garnisons whiche the enemie had thrust in into ruynder lemmer sloten and many other places moe whiche afterward was performed in so muche that all these places were againe restored into the handes of the estates and vnited prouinces vnto whom beseech the lord of his mercie and grace graunt wisedome prouidence and strength daiely more and more to continue their blessed enterprises to the ende thei maie with force resist their enemies prouidently guyde all their affaires and maintaine this debonaire people with all wisedome and equitie and thus gentle reader conclude and ende this present historie reseruyng the reste of the affaires whiche shall succeede for the beginning of an other booke and if it shall please the lord our god to graunt me that his fauour will surely make thee partaker thereof finis a table conteinyng the principall matters conteined within this historie of the troubles and liuill warres in the lowe countreis a tumult in antwerpe spayne in olde tyme gouerned by petie kynges sentence of heretiques souldier killeth his captaine beyng so commaunded by hym souldiers hanged and headed at harlem ibidem spanyolized hollanders letters to leyden spanyolized le hutter writeth to the leydens straunge kindes of meates whiche the leydens vsed scituation of lammen forte spanyardes forsake lammen ibidem schoonhoue rendred spanyardes proclaimed rebelles ibidem the ministers and consistorie purge them selues before the magistrate tournyans discomfited tumult suppressed in antwerpe treatie of the peace at breda citezens ready to resist the assault in steenwike counte rennenberge goeth to viewe the horsemen crueltie of the enemie before steenwike deputie of the estates out of prison dom ihon commeth into the the gantois dom ihon and his adherentes proclaimed open enemies ibidem dom ihon his victorie about giblowe duke of aniowe sendeth to the estates ibidem duke of aniowe his souldiers enter into the englishmen readie to set vpon the towne englishmen driuen of necessitie to eate their horses fascus the colonell found in the habit of a frier fascus by reason of his newe habit is made a laughyng stocke to the whole worlde ibidem ferdinando lopes called the hangman of groenyng franciscanes call againe for fascus his friers weede ibidem fire taketh holde in steenwike gaunt castle besieged and rendred greate counsell of friselande banished hawrech castle taken harlyng castle rendred hope of ayde for steenwike imperiall diet at wormes iesuites and friers packe out of the citie of antwerpe ibidem kyng of spayne ratefieth dom ihon his peace with the estates losy his people appose them selues against colonell robles leeward castle rendred lymbourg besieged and rendred leeward castle besieged and rendred muteny amongest the souldiers at mastright magistrate of arras clapt in prison montigni taketh menine ibidem mastright besieged and wonne menine surprised by the estates nyuell rendreth not one bit of bread left in the towne ordenaunces vpon the pacification of gaune originall of the malcontentes pacification of gaunt prince of oranges protestation prince of orange commeth into brabant prince of orange chosen gouernour of brabant ibidem prelattes and gentlemen taken prisoners at groenyng ibidem phillipuille besieged and rendred peace of the religion publique preachyng throughout all the lowe countreis peace of artois and haynault with the prince of parma pullyng doune of images at leeward robles people make it straunge to be swome vnto hym robles made a prisoner robles his captaines made prisoners request of the estates to the queene of englande sackyng and massacre of antwerpe spanyardes imagine them selues to bee maisters of the lowe countreis spanishe souldiers assemble them selues in braband skirmishe by liege spanyardes driuen to leaue the citie and castle of antwerpe skirmishe harde by louuaine supplication exhibited for the hauyng of the exercise of the religion ibidem substitutes of the citie of antwerpe substitutes of bruges assembled at vight substitutes in flanders assembled at vtright stauere castle rendred siege of steenwike souldiers of steenwike breake the ise steenwikeans skirmishe liuely with the enemie tyrannie of the spanyardes at mastright the companie whiche laie at dam ioyne with them of groening tumult pacified at valencia the tounesmen of steenwike set vp a bande of horsemen they of steenwike make a newe viewe for victualles the enemie chargeth them in the wood the towne reuictualled in the viewe of the enemie the towne againe reuictualled ibidem the siege raised from before steenwike ibidem the siege of steenwike lasted fower whole monethes valencia rendred to the estates vnion of the generall estates vnion of vtright vv westenthorpe the doctor made prisoner waue castle rendred finis
